country_event = {

	id = 19996

	trigger = {
		government = imperium_republic
		any_owned = { 
			civilization_value = 80
			NOT = { religion = THIS }
		}
	}	

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 18
	}	
	
	title = "EVTNAME3111"

	desc = "EVTDESC3111"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3111"				# What a brilliant idea
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		any_owned = {
			limit = { 
				civilization_value = 80 
				NOT = { religion = THIS }
				OR = {
					NOT = { religion = christianity }
					NOT = { religion = judaism }
				}
			}
			religion = THIS
			add_core = THIS
		}
		party = 0
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3111"				# What an awful idea
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		country = {
			set_country_flag = social_war
			set_country_flag = increased_influence
			set_country_flag = riot
		}
		popularity = -5
		party = -1
	}
}

# Loopholes in the law
character_event = {

	id = 19993

	trigger = {
		country = {
			has_country_flag = social_war
			not = { has_country_flag = increased_influence }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 18

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			country = { invention = dissatisfied_plebs }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			country = { stability = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			country = { stability = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			country = { stability = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			country = { 
				ruler = {
					traits = generous
				}
			}
		}
	}	

	title = "EVTNAME3043"

	desc = "EVTDESC3043"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3043"				# Discrete it is
		populist_conviction = 80	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3043"				# It's still a bit risky
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		clr_character_flag = trade_restriction
		clr_character_flag = loopholes
		any_character = {
			loyalty = 70
			wealth = 1000
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 20063

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		NOT = { government = imperium_republic }
		any_character = {
			is_ruler = yes
			NOT = {
				popularity = 100
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5

	}

	title = "popularity"

	desc = "popularity"

	option = {
		name = "popularity"				# Keep the money
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			popularity_change = 80
		}
	}
}

		name = "sell_grain"

	}

		population = 2
	}
}

province_event = {

	id = 20000
	
	trigger = {
		population = 18
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = normalization_of_population_growth }
		owner = {
			government = imperium_republic
			has_country_modifier = major1_military_reform
			has_country_modifier = major2_military_reform
		}		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}	

	title = "EVTNAME4010"
	desc = "EVTDESC4010"

	option = {
		name = "normalization of population growth"	
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = "normalization_of_population_growth"
			duration = 182500
		}
	}
}

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 20008
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	title = "our_religion_must_be_practiced_throughout_our_empire"
	desc = "our_religion_must_be_practiced_throughout_our_empire"

	option = {
		name = "our_religion_must_be_practiced_throughout_our_empire"
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				has_building = temple
				population = 20
				OR = {
					NOT = { religion = THIS }
					NOT = { religion = christianity }
					NOT = { religion = judaism }
				}
			}
			random_list = {	
				60 = { religion = THIS }
				40 = { create_revolt = 10 }
			}
		}
		stability = -6	
	}	
}

country_event = {

	id = 20003
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "imperium republics are a threat"

	desc = "we must not allow other imperium republics the time to grow strong"

	option = {
		name = "sow the seeds of discontent in you neighbor"		#yes mess with their people and leaders 
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {					
				not = { has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms1 }
				not = { alliance_with = THIS }
				government = imperium_republic 
			}			
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "the_people_want_their_freedoms1"
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		treasury = -1000	
	}
	option = {
		name = "invest in our own country"		#no not at this time
		treasury = 150
		add_country_modifier = {
				name = "encourage_our_scientists"
				duration = 740
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 20004
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	title = "we must seek to destroy the neighbors who are not imperium republics also"

	desc = "non imperium republics are still a threat"

	option = {
		name = "we_are_still_weak_but_sow the seeds of discontent in our neighbor"		#yes mess with their people and leaders 
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities = 10
				not = { has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms2 }
				not = { government = imperium_republic }
				not = { alliance_with = THIS }
			}
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "the_people_want_their_freedoms2"
						duration = 1095
					}
				}
				10 = { war = THIS }
			}
		}
		treasury = -1000
	}
	option = {
		name = "we must not create chaos at this time"					#no not at this time
		treasury = 100
		add_country_modifier = {
				name = "encourage_our_youth"
				duration = 740	
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 20018
	
	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			has_building = academy
		}
		has_country_flag = military_academies
		government = imperium_republic
		any_character = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = military_academy }
			prisoner = no
			is_envoy = no
			age = 16
		}	
	}	

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	title = "military academy graduate"
	
	desc = "improved_officer"
	
	option = {
		name = "military academies produce better generals"	
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				is_envoy = no
				NOT = { has_character_flag = military_academy }
			}
			set_character_flag = military_academy
			change_martial = 20
			change_charisma = 20
			change_finesse = 20
		}
	}	

}

country_event = {

	id = 20038
	
	trigger = {	
		any_character = {
			age = 16
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					character_religion = THIS 
					character_religion = christianity 
					character_religion = judaism
				}
			}
		}	
	}	

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	title = "converts_to_state_religion"
	
	desc = "converts_to_state_religion"
	
	option = {
		name = "converts_to_state_religion"	
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				age = 16
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						character_religion = THIS 
						character_religion = christianity 
						character_religion = judaism 
					}
				}
			}
			character_religion = THIS
		}
	}	

}

province_event = {

	id = 20023
	
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			ai = no
			government = imperium_republic
		}
		population = 10
		civilization_value = 50.00
		has_empty_adjacent_province = yes
		any_empty_neighbor_province = {
			barbarian_power = 2
		}
	}

	title = "barbarian_uprising"
	
	desc = "barbarian_uprising"
	
	option = {
		name = "barbarian_uprising"
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		owner = {
			manpower = 15
		}	
		random_empty_neighbor_province = {
			limit = { barbarian_power = 2 }
			barbarian_power = 10
			spawn_horde = 1
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "attempt_to_molify_our_border"
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		owner = {
			treasury = -500
		}
		random_empty_neighbor_province = {
			limit = { barbarian_power = 2 }
			barbarian_power = 4
		}
	}
	
}

		tag = ROM

	}

country_event = {

	id = 20248

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		has_civil_war = no
		war = yes
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { is_civil_war_faction = yes }
		NOT = { stability = -1 }
		any_character = {
			is_ruler = yes
			NOT = { age = 16 }
		}
	
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms1
				has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms2
			}
		}
	}

	title = "to young to rule"

	desc = "to young to rule"

	option = {
		name = "to young to rule"				# Crush them!
		stability = -5
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						barbarian_power = 2
					}
					create_revolt = 15
				}
			}
			35 = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						barbarian_power = 2
					}
					random_list = {
						55 = { barbarian_create_client = yes }
						45 = {
							barbarian_power = 9
							spawn_horde = 1
						}
						
					}
				
				}
			}
			25 = {
				random_character = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						is_ruler = no
						is_governor = yes
						location = { 
							owned_by = THIS 
							controlled_by = THIS
						} 
					}
					start_civil_war = yes
					set_character_flag = rebel_side
					character_event = 9006
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 20249
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	title = "support_rebellion"

	desc = "support_rebellion"

	option = {
		name = "support_rebellion"		#yes mess with their people and leaders 
		treasury = -4900
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "we_are_shifty"
			duration = 1800 
		}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				has_civil_war = no
				num_of_cities = 80
				NOT = { is_civil_war_faction = yes }
				NOT = { alliance_with = THIS }
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms1
						has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms2
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = 20250
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 20251
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { exists = SED }
		owns = 16
        OR = {
			has_civil_war = yes 
			is_civil_war_faction = yes
		} 
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

		months = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			ruler = {
				NOT = { age = 16}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 521
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 654
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			year = 704
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			ruler = { military = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			ruler = { military = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			ruler = { military = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			ruler = { military = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			not = { stability = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			not = { stability = -2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				owner = { government = imperium_republic }
			}
		}
	}

	title = "sedentani independence"
	desc = "sedentani independence"


	option = {
		name = "sedentani independence"					# Let them be for now...		
		16 = { secede_province = SED }
		SED = { 
			add_core = 16
			country_event = 20292 
		}
	}
}

			limit = {				
				not = { has_country_modifier = the_people_want_their_freedoms2 }

				num_of_cities = 8
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "the_people_want_their_freedoms2"
						duration = 1095
					}
				}
				30 = { war = THIS }
			}
		}
		treasury = -1000
	}
	option = {
		name = "we must not create chaos at this time"					#no not at this time
		treasury = 100
		add_country_modifier = {
				name = "encourage_our_youth"
				duration = 740	
		}
	}

			}

country_event = {

	id = 20567
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = governors_are_prickly
		has_civil_war = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

		months = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			ruler = {
				NOT = { age = 16}
			}
		}
	}

	title = "civil_war"
	desc = "civil_war"


	option = {
		name = "civil_war"					# Let them be for now...		
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_ruler = no
				OR = {
					is_governor = yes
					is_general = yes
				}
				location = { 
					owned_by = THIS 
					controlled_by = THIS
				} 
			}
			start_civil_war = yes
			set_character_flag = rebel_side
			character_event = 9006
		}
	}
}
